                            <script>
                            $(document).ready(function () {
                                var $ozelOption = $('.variant-list-group .variant-text[data-option-title="Özel Kumaş Seçimi"]').first();
                                if (!$ozelOption.length) return;

                                var viewer = document.getElementById('modelViewer');
                                if (!viewer) return;

                                $('.product-customization-group[data-group-id="2"]').hide();

                                var ozelOptionTitle = $ozelOption.attr('data-option-title');
                                var currentProductId = 80244;
                                var fabricSelection = null;

                                var CHILDREN = [
                                                                    ];

                                var ozelChildren = CHILDREN.filter(function (c) {
                                    return c.name && c.name.indexOf(ozelOptionTitle) > -1;
                                });
                                var onOzelChild = ozelChildren.some(function (c) { return c.id === currentProductId; });

                                // IdeaSoft varyant AJAX navigasyonu Sugar viewer'ı yeniden başlatamıyor; full reload'a çeviriyoruz.
                                try {
                                    if (ozelChildren.length && typeof IdeaApp !== 'undefined' && IdeaApp.product && IdeaApp.product.variant && !IdeaApp.product.variant._loadContentPatched) {
                                        IdeaApp.product.variant.loadContent = function (url) { window.location.href = url; };
                                        IdeaApp.product.variant._loadContentPatched = true;
                                    }
                                } catch (err) {}

                                $('head').append(
                                    '<style>' +
                                    '.variant-text[data-option-title="Özel Kumaş Seçimi"] {cursor:pointer !important;color:#FFF !important;background-color:#114b96 !important;border-color:#114b96 !important;}' +
                                    '.variant-text[data-option-title="Özel Kumaş Seçimi"]:hover {background-color:#0c3468 !important;border-color:#0c3468 !important;color:#FFF !important;}' +
                                    '.variant-text[data-option-title="Özel Kumaş Seçimi"].fabric-open {background-color:#f8bc25 !important;border-color:#f8bc25 !important;color:#000 !important;}' +
                                    '.variant-text[data-option-title="Özel Kumaş Seçimi"].fabric-open:hover {background-color:#e0a820 !important;border-color:#e0a820 !important;color:#000 !important;}' +
                                    '#fabric-selection {position:relative;}' +
                                    '#fabric-selection-close {position:absolute;top:8px;right:8px;width:28px;height:28px;line-height:28px;text-align:center;border-radius:50%;background:#114b96;color:#FFF;cursor:pointer;font-weight:700;z-index:5;user-select:none;}' +
                                    '#fabric-selection-close:hover {background:#0c3468;}' +
                                    '</style>'
                                );

                                var $fabricDiv = $('<div id="fabric-selection" style="display:none;"><span id="fabric-selection-close" title="Kapat">X</span><div id="fabric-selection-content"></div></div>');
                                $('.product-options').after($fabricDiv);

                                var $variantPlural = $('.variant-plural');
                                var isOpen = false;

                                function openFabric() {
                                    isOpen = true;
                                    $ozelOption.addClass('fabric-open');
                                    $variantPlural.slideUp(300);
                                    $fabricDiv.slideDown(300);
                                    $('.ar-thumb-item a').trigger('click');
                                }

                                function closeFabric() {
                                    isOpen = false;
                                    $ozelOption.removeClass('fabric-open');
                                    $variantPlural.slideDown(300);
                                    $fabricDiv.slideUp(300);
                                    $('#product-thumb-image .thumb-item:not(.ar-thumb-item):first a').trigger('click');
                                }

                                $fabricDiv.on('click', '#fabric-selection-close', closeFabric);

                                $ozelOption.on('click', function (e) {
                                    if (onOzelChild) {
                                        e.stopImmediatePropagation();
                                        e.preventDefault();
                                        isOpen ? closeFabric() : openFabric();
                                        return;
                                    }
                                    if (ozelChildren.length === 1 && ozelChildren[0].url) {
                                        e.stopImmediatePropagation();
                                        e.preventDefault();
                                        window.location.href = ozelChildren[0].url;
                                    }
                                });

                                viewer.addEventListener('dataload', function (e) {
                                    if (e.detail && e.detail.gltf && onOzelChild && !isOpen) openFabric();
                                });

                                viewer.addEventListener('material-zone-updated', function (e) {
                                    fabricSelection = e.detail;
                                    syncCustomizationInput(null);
                                });

                                function readZonesFromDom() {
                                    return $('#fabric-selection .sugar-mz-fab__row').map(function () {
                                        return {
                                            label: $(this).find('.sugar-mz-fab__row-label').text().trim(),
                                            name: $(this).find('.sugar-mz-fab__pill-name').text().trim()
                                        };
                                    }).get();
                                }

                                function zonesValid() {
                                    var zones = readZonesFromDom();
                                    return zones.length > 0 && zones.every(function (z) { return z.name; });
                                }

                                function captureAndStoreImage() {
                                    try {
                                        if (typeof viewer.takeOppositeProductScreenShot !== 'function') return null;
                                        var rect = viewer.getBoundingClientRect();
                                        var dataUrl = viewer.takeOppositeProductScreenShot(
                                            Math.round(rect.width) || 600,
                                            Math.round(rect.height) || 400
                                        );
                                        if (!dataUrl) return null;
                                        var key = 'fabricImg_' + Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8);
                                        sessionStorage.setItem(key, dataUrl);
                                        return key;
                                    } catch (err) { return null; }
                                }

                                function buildCustomizationText(imgKey) {
                                    var parts = [];
                                    if (fabricSelection && fabricSelection.zonesResult && fabricSelection.zonesResult.sku) {
                                        parts.push('Kumaş SKU: ' + fabricSelection.zonesResult.sku);
                                    }
                                    var zones = readZonesFromDom();
                                    if (zones.length) {
                                        parts.push('Bölgeler: ' + zones.map(function (z) { return z.label + ': ' + z.name; }).join(', '));
                                    }
                                    if (imgKey) parts.push('[IMG:' + imgKey + ']');
                                    return parts.join(' | ') || 'Özel Kumaş Seçimi';
                                }

                                function syncCustomizationInput(imgKey) {
                                    $('.product-customization-group[data-group-id="2"] input[data-selector="customization-form-field"]').val(buildCustomizationText(imgKey));
                                }

                                document.addEventListener('click', function (ev) {
                                    if (!onOzelChild) return;
                                    var target = ev.target.closest && ev.target.closest('.add-to-cart-button[data-selector="add-to-cart"]');
                                    if (!target) return;

                                    if (!zonesValid()) {
                                        ev.preventDefault();
                                        ev.stopImmediatePropagation();
                                        alert('Lütfen tüm kumaş bölgeleri için seçim yapınız.');
                                        return;
                                    }

                                    syncCustomizationInput(captureAndStoreImage());
                                }, true);
                            });
                            </script>

  function reinitLiveChat() {
      if (window.location.pathname !== "/sepet") {
          try {
              const liveChatElements = document.querySelectorAll('[id*="liveChat"], [class*="liveChat"], [id*="infobip"]');
              liveChatElements.forEach(element => {
                  if (element && element.parentNode) {
                      element.parentNode.removeChild(element);
                  }
              });

              if (window.liveChat) {
                  delete window.liveChat;
              }

              setTimeout(() => {
                  (function(I,n,f,o,b,i,p){
                      I[b]=I[b]||function(){(I[b].q=I[b].q||[]).push(arguments)};
                      I[b].t=1*new Date();i=n.createElement(f);i.async=1;i.src=o;

                      if (typeof window.liveChat === 'function') {
                          liveChat('init', '3983827b-bf89-44c8-b977-6b4f4d4eb72f');
                      }
                  }, 200);

              }, 500);

          } catch (error) {
              console.log('LiveChat error:', error);
          }
      }
  }

  $(document).ready(function() {
      $(document).on('click', '[data-selector="select-plural-variant"] span', function() {
          setTimeout(() => {
              reinitLiveChat();
          }, 1000);
      });
  });

<script>
(function() {
  var supportsPassive = eventListenerOptionsSupported();  

  if (supportsPassive) {
    var addEvent = EventTarget.prototype.addEventListener;
    overwriteAddEvent(addEvent);
  }

  function overwriteAddEvent(superMethod) {
    var defaultOptions = {
      passive: true,
      capture: false
    };

    EventTarget.prototype.addEventListener = function(type, listener, options) {
      var usesListenerOptions = typeof options === 'object';
      var useCapture = usesListenerOptions ? options.capture : options;

      options = usesListenerOptions ? options : {};
      options.passive = options.passive !== undefined ? options.passive : defaultOptions.passive;
      options.capture = useCapture !== undefined ? useCapture : defaultOptions.capture;

      superMethod.call(this, type, listener, options);
    };
  }

  function eventListenerOptionsSupported() {
    var supported = false;
    try {
      var opts = Object.defineProperty({}, 'passive', {
        get: function() {
          supported = true;
        }
      });
      window.addEventListener("test", null, opts);
    } catch (e) {}

    return supported;
